October 10, 2005 Monday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"'US' magazine reporting that Jessica Simpson and Nick Lachey have split up. ... See, this kind of thing really upsets me. We knew Nick and Jessica were having problems months ago. And did FEMA do anything?"

Jay Leno:

"President Bush's top adviser Karl Rove will be testifying for the fourth time before a grand jury at the Federal courthouse in Washington next week. You know, Maybe Bush should nominate him to the Supreme Court. He's been in more courtrooms than Harriet Miers now, pretty much." 

Jay Leno:

"I tell you the Republicans are having their problems. Karl Rove testifying, as said, for the fourth time next week. Tom DeLay indicted for the second time. Bill Frist being investigated. You know, for a party that hates trial lawyers, they sure do hire a lot of them, don't they?"

Jay Leno:

"Homeland Security officials are now telling people in New York City to be on the lookout for men traveling alone and speaking a foreign language. That's pretty much the Yankees' pitching staff, isn't it?"

Jay Leno:

"The good news, the threat is not as bad as they thought yesterday. Today the Mayor of New York City wanted to reassure New Yorkers. He said the New York City subways are still safe to urinate in."

Jay Leno:

"President Bush today called those who support terrorism evil but not insane. As opposed to those people who just bought an SUV. They're insane but not evil."

Jay Leno

: "As you may have heard, oil, now under $60 a barrel. You know what this means for the American consumer? Nothing."

Jay Leno:

"They had a full page ad from the oil and gas industry in the paper today -- explaining to us, you know, it says where does the dollar you pay for a gallon of gas go? Well, 54 cents towards the crude oil. 30 cents to refining transportation. And 16 cents goes to taxes. Here's my question, where do you get a gallon of gas for a dollar?"

Jay Leno

: "What's the other $2.50? That's pretty all much profit."

Jay Leno:

"In what's being called the first case of espionage in the White House in modern history -- this is pretty serious -- a former Marine that who worked for Vice President Dick Cheney at the White House being accused of stealing top secret information and passing it on. And you know the sad part about this, the guy accused of spying, he was Bush's second choice for Supreme Court nominee."

Jay Leno:

"Actually, President Bush's number one choice, Harriet Miers, issued a statement today saying she's getting closer and closer to having an opinion on something."

Jay Leno:

"See, this is interesting, conservatives on the far right are mad at President Bush for nominating Harriet Miers. And liberals are still mad at him for nominating John Roberts. So he is a uniter, not a divider. No, he's done the impossible. He's got both conservatives and liberals teamed up against him. You know how hard that is to do?"

Jay Leno:

"If you're wondering how Harriet Miers got the nomination, she probably saw this ad. Take a look." Ad announcer: "Tired of working at a dead end job? Wish you do more with your life? Well, now you can, at the George W. Bush Institute for Supreme Court judges. You'll soon discover that interpreting constitutional law has never been easier. No experience is necessary. In fact, it's not even encouraged. So trade in that hairnet and name tag for a long, black robe and become a Supreme Court judge by enrolling at the George W. Bush Institute for Supreme Court judges. Easy financing is available."

Jay Leno:

"The former FBI Director, Louis Freeh has a new book out. I think he's on 60 Minutes Sunday. He goes after President Clinton. He says that Clinton's closets were full of skeletons. Skeletons? So I guess there were some skinny chicks we didn't know about."

Jay Leno:

"According to the Wall Street Journal, we may soon be able to vote in our elections by telephone. You can vote by telephone. Don't have to go to the voting booth anymore. This is using a law passed in 2002 called the 'American Idol' Act that allows you to vote by phone."

Jay Leno:

"The Defense Department is having a race for robotic vehicles across the desert. Any kind of vehicle that can be driven by remote control can compete for the $2 million prize. So far the top contender is a Hummer driven by a robot, or as we call that -- the Governor of California."

David Letterman:

"Speaking of the fall television season, I don't think it is going that well for NBC. Earlier today, President Bush made his fourth trip to the set of 'Joey.'"

David Letterman:

"Have you heard about this, President Bush has nominated Harriet Miers to the Supreme Court. And this very, very important. She's a member of the president's inner circle. That is how they describe her. She has never really been a judge before but they describe her as an important member of the president's inner circle. That means she's his designated driver."

Conan O'Brien:

"Yesterday, Supreme Court nominee Harriet Miers told reporters, this is a quote, 'President Bush is the most brilliant man I've ever met.' That's a quote, yeah. Actually, the entire quote was, 'President Bush is the most brilliant man I've ever met who still eats paste.'"

October 11, 2005 Tuesday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Happy Columbus Day, everybody. The holiday named, of course, for the man who discovered America. Although President Bush said Columbus didn't really occupy the country so much as liberate the Indians."

Jay Leno:

"Columbus did not set out to discover America. No, no, no. He was looking for a quicker route to India. You know why he was trying to get to India? Anybody know? He was trying to get the King of Spain's computer fixed." 

Jay Leno:

"See, actually, Columbus Day is quite controversial. This is a day of celebration for Italians, but it offends a lot of Native Americans. But see, I can understand both points of view. That's why I'm a very open person. I try to honor both. Like every Columbus Day, I go to an Indian casino and have a big Italian dinner."

Jay Leno:

"Most medical historians now believe it was Christopher Columbus who brought sexually transmitted diseases to the new world. But on the other hand, the Indians gave him tobacco. So it's pretty much a wash."

Jay Leno:

"US relief supplies have already started arriving in Pakistan. That's pretty quick, huh? I didn't realize Pakistan was so much closer to the United States than New Orleans."

Jay Leno:

"And it was reported today that troops may stay on in New Orleans through next year. Next year there will be troops in New Orleans. Pretty amazing, isn't it? Not only does Bush not have an exit strategy for Iraq, we don't even have one for New Orleans."

Jay Leno:

"Over the weekend, a huge wildfire jumped across the border from Mexico to California. Here is the really strange part -- today it got a job at Wal-Mart."

Jay Leno:

"Rain, major flooding all over New Hampshire. Bridges collapsed, roads were washed out. In fact it prompted Kanye West to say President Bush doesn't care about the one black guy that lives in New Hampshire."

Jay Leno:

"More news on that spy they arrested who was working in Vice President Dick Cheney's office. Did you hear about that story? Pretty amazing. Turns out he started working at the White House during the Clinton Administration. Well, duh. I mean, where do you think he learned how to sneak around without getting caught? He learned from the best."

Jay Leno:

"Security has been increased on all New York City subways after authorities received a word of a terrorist threat. Officials here in LA also calling for increased security on LA subways as soon as we can figure out where the hell they are."

Jay Leno:

"Anybody looking for a job in TV? Did you hear this? Al Qaeda is hiring. I'm not making this up. On its website, al Qaeda is looking to hire people for video production work. It's for young people who are terrorists who really want to direct, basically."

Jay Leno:

"Al Qaeda is looking for people. And they have several -- they said 'Vacant positions available.' I imagine if one of your most common entry level positions is suicide bomber, there's going to be a lot of openings."

Jay Leno:

"President Bush's top adviser Karl Rove will be testifying for the fourth time, fourth time before the grand jury at the Federal courthouse in Washington this week. And President Bush's Supreme Court nominee, Harriet Miers, is fascinated by all this. Today she asked Rove, 'What goes on in those Federal courthouses anyways?'"

Jay Leno:

"We don't know a lot about this Harriet Miers, but she told the New York Times, she said that George Bush was the most brilliant man she ever met. You know, this chick's got to meet more guys."

Jay Leno:

"The Air Force is now developing a non-lethal microwave ray that they can fire at enemy ground troops. They would literally microwave the enemy through this ray. Very sophisticated, too, and it has different settings for different countries. Like Turkey, you set it to high for 15 minutes. Chinese, you put it on reheat."

Jay Leno:

"Some researchers now believe fat can be used as a source of stem cells. They can use fat. Well, that should secure America's lead in stem cell research, huh?"

Jay Leno:

"Stem cells from fat may one day be used to cure a number of diseases. Your fat ass may one day save your fat ass."

Jay Leno:

"Today, Federal health officials issued new warnings about the bird flu. They say be on the lookout for weak, sickly looking birds like the Philadelphia Eagle, a bird that's not able to protect itself."

David Letterman:

"Columbus Day here in New York City, and the new terror alert color is marinara."

David Letterman:

"On Friday, Mayor Bloomberg said, there may be trouble, things to look for. There may be a bag here, look at the bag there. They put on 1,000 extra cops. Thank God everything turned out, it was all right. But yesterday, I'm on the subway, and security was unbelievably tight. And a guy comes up to me and says, take off your pants. And I said, I said, 'Are you from Homeland Security?' And he said, 'No I just want to settle a bet.'"

David Letterman:

"How about that Harriet Miers? Who wants to be a Supreme Court judge? Fill out the application as you leave the theater tonight."

David Letterman:

"And Harriet Miers, so yesterday she goes to church, and at her church she receives a standing ovation. Harriet Miers gets a standing ovation. She is an inspiration to unqualified people everywhere."

David Letterman:

"And now it's the all-important background check into Harriet Miers, and I'm thinking, 'Oh, I hope they don't find out about our weekend in Atlantic City, because that was Katie-bar-the-door.'"

David Letterman:

"Harriet is the...I think she is the most controversial Supreme Court pick since, well, since George Bush."

HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Security was beefed up in the subway system in New York again today. Not because of terrorist threats. Yankee fans were throwing themselves in front of a train."

"That security scare in the New York city subway turned out to be nothing. Turned out to be a hoax. In fact, officials now say it is now okay to go back to your usual, normal, everyday fear of riding the subway. The stabbings, the muggings -- whew! Thank God things are back to normal."

"The FBI says they're now considering relaxing their drug policy on new applicants that want to join the FBI. If you smoke marijuana, it's ok. You thought the FBI was losing stuff before -- oh, my gosh. How bad will it be when they're high on weed now? So much for the war on drugs."

Jay Leno:

"That's the FBI's new policy. If you can't beat them, join them, apparently."

Jay Leno:

"The FBI will not hire you if you smoked pot more than 15 times in your life. Not today. You cannot join if you smoke marijuana more than 15 times. But the good news -- you can still be President."

Jay Leno:

"How do they come up with this? Who picked the number 15? I mean, after a guy smoked dope 8, 10 to 13 times, it's pretty obvious that he likes it, right? A lot of stoners going, 'Oh, this is my 14th joint. No more for me, dude. I'm joining the FBI.'"

Jay Leno:

"Harriet Miers -- you know, the Supreme Court nominee -- she told the New York Times President Bush is the most brilliant man she knows, and Vice President Dick Cheney, the greatest athlete she's ever met."

Jay Leno:

"No, Newsweek reports that President Bush likes Harriet Miers because she didn't go to an Ivy League school, she worked hard and she's achieved everything on her own without family help. So, see that, opposites attract."

Jay Leno:

"Well, the latest rumor is, she has so few supporters that her nomination will be withdrawn. They're saying they're gonna withdraw it. They think Bush may have to go to the woman who has had more courtroom experience. You know, like Courtney Love."

Jay Leno:

"As you know, yesterday, we celebrated Columbus Day. Did you know Columbus died penniless? Did you know this? He died completely broke. You know what happened? Before he returned to Spain, he stopped off at an Indian casino, lost everything."

Jay Leno:

"And as you know, there's terrible flooding in New Hampshire. It's been declared a disaster area. To give you an idea how white New Hampshire is, FEMA got there in a minute and a half. Okay?"

Jay Leno:

"A woman from New Orleans who lost her house in Hurricane Katrina hit the $1.6 million slot machine jackpot at the casino in Louisiana. And here's the amazing part. Within an hour of her winning, Federal officials were down there, giving her tax forms to fill out. Huh? Where were these people when her house got washed away?"

Jay Leno:

"Over the weekend, Hillary Clinton was inducted into the national Women's Hall of Fame. Quite an honor. However, she is still not in Bill Clinton's women's hall of fame. In fact, she's not even in the top ten."

Jay Leno:

"Well, it's official. The new James Bond is actor Daniel Craig. Daniel Craig is the new James Bond. Even Harriet Miers is going, 'Who's Daniel Craig?'"

David Letterman:

"Congratulations to Bill and Hillary Clinton. It's their 30th wedding anniversary today. Bill showed up at the scene of his wedding with former President Bush."

David Letterman:

"And I thought this was nice. Last night, Bill put together a lovely anniversary celebration. It was a quiet, candlelight dinner for two at a beautiful seaside hotel. And I don't know where Hillary was but..."

David Letterman:

"I don't know if you heard this late-breaking bulletin. Earlier today, President Bush has pledged to rebuild the Yankees no matter what the cost."

Conan O'Brien:

"The White House is denying a report from the BBC that claims that President Bush said God told him to invade Iraq. Yeah. He's denying it. President Bush denied the report and said, 'That's not true. I invaded Iraq because Batman told me to.'"

The Frontrunner


June 6, 2006 Tuesday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"President Bush gave his weekly radio address on Saturday and the theme was 'pro-marriage.' And then right afterwards, President Clinton gave the rebuttal." 

Jay Leno:

"President Bush calling for an amendment against gay marriage. Or as President Bush calls it, 'Leave that fellow's behind.'"

Jay Leno:

"Do we need an amendment? Is that the most important issue facing the country today? Gay marriage? You know, we were off last week. So apparently, we must have caught bin Laden. Did I miss that story?"

Jay Leno:

"According to a poll, 51% of Americans do not approve of gay marriage, but 70% of Americans do not approve of President Bush. Gay marriage is actually more popular than he is."

Jay Leno:

"Did you notice, gay marriage didn't become a big Republican priority until all their members started going to prison?"

Jay Leno:

"Donald Rumsfeld was in Vietnam this week. President Bush was supposed to go with him. But his dad got him out of it."

Jay Leno:

"This weekend, a person was caught trying to jump over the White House fence after throwing a package over it. Turns out, it was just Hillary Clinton with carpet samples. But it was scary."

Jay Leno:

"Oh, how annoying is this? Senator Hillary Clinton, calling for a return of the 55 miles an hour speed limit? When people in LA heard about this, they went, 'What? Cars can go that fast?'"

Jay Leno:

"Honda has announced it developed technology that links a person's thoughts to a machine, uses brain signals to control a robot's movements. To which Al Gore said, 'Been there, done that.'"

David Letterman:

"Homeland Security is cutting funding for New York City and raising funding for Nebraska. Well, at least the corn sleep better."

David Letterman:

"The Canadian Mounties, they busted a group of Canadian terrorists. Canadian al Qaeda group, about 19 of them. They busted, their motto was 'Death to America, eh.'"

David Letterman:

"The Canadian terrorist group was lead by Canadian mastermind Gordie bin Laden."

David Letterman:

"Yesterday a guy hopped the fence at the White House. Pretty scary. Thank God at the last minute Dick Cheney picked him off."

David Letterman:

"Top Ten Surprises In Al Gore's Global Warming Movie: 10. The role of Al Gore Is played by Bruce Willis.

9. During the summer months, Al and Tipper host nude barbecues.

8. Hilarious outtake of Al Gore saying 'wobal glarming.'

7. It's a musical.

6. Refers to Arizona as being 'hotter than Tipper's ass.'

5. Claims global warming melted Kenny Rogers' face.

4. Blames the crisis on a creepy albino.

3. The scientist who supports all of his claims is Al Gore in a mustache.

2. Best solution is to contribute heavily to Al-Gore-In-2008.com.

1. It feels longer than the Florida recount."

June 7, 2006 Wednesday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Today was also Election Day in California, or, as we call it in Los Angeles, 'Tuesday.'"

Jay Leno:

"The election day in California is the start of the process where we elect the next leader of the Mexican people."

Jay Leno: 

"US fighter jets intercepted a small plane that had breached restricted airspace around Washington. Did you hear about that? Apparently, the White House said not to shoot it down unless they had evidence that it contained two gay guys who wanted to get married."

Jay Leno:

"As you know, President Bush calling for a constitutional amendment against gay marriage. He says he wants to put both al Qaeda and Ikea out of business."

Jay Leno:

"Some were surprised that President Bush would back a gay marriage amendment, when it clearly doesn't have the votes to pass. But are you surprised by that? I mean, since when has a lack of votes held back President Bush?"

Jay Leno:

"Even though President Bush is pressing for this gay marriage amendment, Vice President Dick Cheney says he doesn't think the Federal Government should be involved. Yeah. Cheney said the government shouldn't prevent men who are obviously in love with each other from having a relationship. For example, let's say the head of an oil company wants to get in bed with the leader of the Republican Party. They should be allowed."

Jay Leno:

"This past weekend, the Secret Service arrested a guy for trying to jump the fence at the White House. Again! Think about this. They want to build a fence along the Mexican border? We can't even build a fence around the White House to keep people from jumping over!"

Jay Leno:

"Congressman Patrick Kennedy was released from rehab this week. In fact, they took precautions in Washington. They placed concrete barriers in front of the concrete barriers."

Jay Leno:

"Actually, Kennedy was not cured, the doctors made him leave. They said, 'Cure a Kennedy? Hey, we're doctors, not miracle workers!'"

Jay Leno:

"After coming out of rehab, Congressman Patrick Kennedy said he wants to be treated 'just like a black man, if and when he gets charged for crashing his car into Capitol Hill.' That's what he said. He wants to be treated the same as a black man, yeah. He said that, six cops jumped him, beat the hell out of him."

Jay Leno:

"He said, 'I want to be treated like a black guy,' and then every black guy said, 'Hey, forget that, how about treating us like a rich white guy?'"

Jay Leno:

"According to Life and Style Weekly,' Britney Spears' marriage to Kevin has basically turned into a business deal. That's what they said. They said he pretends to be a good husband, and not embarrass her in public, and then he can go out on weekends and do whatever he wants. I'm sorry, that's Bill and Hillary's deal. I'm sorry."

David Letterman:

"Ladies and gentlemen, here in New York, city gun violence in New York city is up 12%. I knew we could turn this thing around."

David Letterman:

"Honestly, quite a lot of gun play now in New York City, but I don't mind. It's a good workout dodging sporadic sniper fire."

David Letterman:

"Well, the big World Cup tournament kicks off in Germany and they start with a big parade. The giant parade of nations that hate America."

David Letterman:

"Yesterday, I guess it was a big scare down there in Washington DC, a small plane violated White House air space. And the incident was very upsetting to the President. He was really concerned because he's in the White House at the time and a plane...and here's the problem. He thought it was coming to take him on vacation so he was really upset."

David Letterman:

"But thank God, the resolution to the thing had a happy outcome because at the last minute Dick Cheney picked it off."

David Letterman:

"Top Ten Signs It May Be The Apocalypse: 10. Gas is now $6.66 a gallon.

9. Earlier today George W. Bush correctly pronounced 'apocalypse.'

8. The minute you finish washing your car, it starts raining, am I right, people? You know what I'm talking about.

7. On tonight's 'Anderson Cooper 360,' his head spun around 360 degrees.

6. At lunch, my alphabet soup spelled, 'Eat it.'

5. People are actually buying a razor with five blades.

4. Two words: Governor Schwarzenegger.

3. While getting dressed, you discover pitchfork marks on your ass.

2. Kenny Rogers knows when to hold 'em and fold 'em, but not when to walk away from the plastic surgeon.

1. The Mets are in first place."

Conan O'Brien:

"Yesterday, the Secret Service caught a man trying to climb over the White House fence. ... Yeah, when they caught the man, the Secret Service said, 'Not so fast. You have three more years, Mr. President.'"

Conan O'Brien:

President Bush gave his speech about illegal immigration. Yeah. In his speech, the President told the people of New Mexico, 'We'll never let you into our country.'"

Conan O'Brien:

"The Senate is considering a constitutional amendment that would ban gay marriage. That's right. Yeah. The amendment is expected to fall a few votes short because Senators Orrin Hatch and Trent Lott are antiquing in Vermont."

Conan O'Brien:

"This week, Congressman Patrick Kennedy left rehab and returned to Rhode Island. He left rehab and returned to Rhode Island. Unfortunately on his way back, he hit Massachusetts, Connecticut and New Hampshire."

June 8, 2006 Thursday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"That's right, 6/6/06, the devil did not show up yesterday, how about that. Unless, of course, you're a Democrat watching Ann Coulter on the Today show."

Jay Leno:

"Yesterday was election day in California. A record-low turnout, 28%. See, that's what happens when the candidates are named Phil Angelides and Steve Westly, instead of Taylor Hicks and Katharine McPhee." 

Jay Leno:

"The Senate has rejected the gay marriage ban. If you think about it, you really want Congress defining marriage? That's like asking Charlie Sheen to define monogamy, isn't it?"

Jay Leno:

"Republican leaders say that after illegal immigration and gay marriage, the next issue President Bush will tackle, flag burning. Flag burning. So, if you're an illegal immigrant who's crossing our border to burn the flag at your gay wedding, we got your number."

Jay Leno:

"Vice President Dick Cheney gave the commencement speech at his old high school in Casper, Wyoming, last weekend. He told graduating seniors to aim high, because if they didn't, they might shoot somebody in the face."

Jay Leno:

"According to the Center for Public Integrity, in the last five years, Congress got $50 million worth of free trips. $50 million. Isn't that unbelievable? That's over 23,000 free trips. Paid for by somebody else. Yeah. That beats the old record set by Kevin Federline."

Jay Leno:

"On the current record charts, Dixie Chicks now have the number one album in the country. More bad news for President Bush."

David Letterman:

"Big vote in the Senate yesterday. They voted down the gay marriage ban. ... It was a very close vote, 43 voted yea, 44 voted nay, and three voted fabulous."

David Letterman:

"Now the Vatican says that gay marriage actually is threatening family, threatening families. Really? More than priests?"

David Letterman:

Ann Coulter "goes around yakking, and she's got herself in a lot of trouble. She made some crazy statements about 9/11. And coincidentally -- and you wouldn't believe this, but coincidentally, Al Gore has now produced a new documentary all about Ann Coulter. It's crazy. Yeah. I believe it's called 'An Inconvenient Bitch.'"

David Letterman:

"But here's what we know about Ann Coulter. She's blond, and she's single, and, well, well, maybe somebody will set her up with OJ."

Conan O'Brien:

"Yesterday, Yankees outfielder Melky Cabrera made a spectacular catch...against the left field fence to defeat the Red Sox. And he went up and over. It was incredible. Experts say it's the first time all year a Hispanic man's been cheered for leaping over a fence."

Conan O'Brien:

"Yesterday, President Bush went to Nebraska and gave a big speech about immigration. Yeah. Of course, to people in Nebraska, 'immigration' means 'moving to Iowa.'"

Conan O'Brien:

"Next week, 88-year-old Senator Robert Byrd will become the longest-serving US senator in American history. Yeah, 88. That's crazy. When asked if he was still capable of conducting the business of state, the 88- year-old Senator said, 'I like lemons.'"

June 9, 2006 Friday


HEADLINE: Late Night Political Humor


BODY:

Jay Leno:

"Well, the big story, as you probably know, yesterday US forces killed terrorist al Zarqawi in an air strike. We didn't get the devil on 06/06/06, but we only missed it by one day. That's not bad."

Jay Leno: 

"He was hit by two 500-pound bombs. Now, al Zarqawi's name is now Ow, Ow, Ow Zarqawi."

Jay Leno:

"You know what his last words were? Holy Shiite."

Jay Leno:

"To give you an idea of how dangerous things are in Iraq, do you know where Zarqawi was when he was killed? In a safe house."

Jay Leno:

"I think Zarqawi knew what his fate was going to be. Like, today they just released his autobiography. Coincidentally, it's called, 'I'm in a million little pieces.'"

Jay Leno:

"Discussing the incident today, Secretary of Defense Donald Rumsfeld said, 'Al Zarqawi was mean, vicious and hateful.' So, you know what that means? Ann Coulter could be next."

Jay Leno:

"A Federal Air Marshal has been suspended from his job after appearing on the TV show 20/20 to complain that the government isn't doing enough job of protecting the identities of Air Marshals. He went on TV to complain that the government was not keeping his identity a secret."

Jay Leno:

"It was so hot" in California, "Dick Cheney went to see al gore's movie, just for the air conditioning."

Jay Leno:

"It was so hot, gay couples were standing next to President Bush, just to get the cold shoulder."

Jay Leno:

"Yesterday, President Bush gave a big speech on immigration in Nebraska. And really, what better place to talk about border problems than Nebraska?"

Jay Leno:

"Al Gore on the show tonight, ladies and gentlemen. This just shows you how quickly things can change. I mean, Arnold Schwarzenegger spends his days talking about his political agenda. Al Gore is out promoting his new movie."

Jay Leno:

"Did you know Al Gore was voted our second most popular guest ever? Actually he finished first, but the Supreme Court, they overturned..."

Jay Leno:

"A lot of people say Al Gore was the best vice president the country ever had. Now, not to take anything away from Al, but look at the competition. Okay? He replaced a guy who couldn't spell potato. And he was followed by a guy who shot someone in the face."

Jay Leno:

"Al Gore's movie about global warming broke into the top ten this past weekend. And President Bush was not impressed. He said, 'My movie about me, 'Fahrenheit 9/11,' did better than that.'"

Jay Leno:

"President Bush said he's not going to see the film. He's not going to go see it. He said he did go see Ice Age II: The Meltdown, so he has all of the facts about global warming."

Jay Leno:

"Al Gore's movie, 'An Inconvenient Truth,' it made about $2 million this past weekend. Whereas 'X-Men' made about $150 million. That just goes to show you, we're more interested in fake people trying to save the fake earth, than real people trying to save the real earth."

Jay Leno:

"Actually, pretty sobering film. I saw it. The critics were calling it a wake-up call. Which is amazing. Whoever thought Al Gore would be giving people a wake-up call?"

Jay Leno:

"He makes some interesting points in the film. He says global warming is so bad, they have actually detected a thaw between Bill and Hillary."

Jay Leno:

"They also said if global warming continues tropical countries to the south will become too hot to live in and their desperate citizens will flee north. Which means millions of Mexicans could sneak into the United States. Oh, like that would ever happen."

David Letterman:

"I have been thinking about this. Do you think it is too soon to hit on Mrs. Zarqawi?"

David Letterman:

"You heard go this, of course, Abu Musab al Zarqawi is dead. Nice shot, Cheney."

David Letterman:

"Abu Musab al Zarqawi was the world's most unhinged lunatic. He is now dead so, that moves Ann Coulter up to first place."

Conan O'Brien:

"It was announced today that the US military dropped a bomb that killed Iraq's number one terrorist, Abu Musab al Zarqawi. They got rid of Abu Musab al Zarqawi. Yeah. Afterwards, President Bush said, 'Oh, great, and I just learned how to pronounce his name.'"

Conan O'Brien:

"They got al Zarqawi while he was hiding in his safe house. Yeah. As a result, it's been renamed the 'Not-so-safe house.'"

She goes to visit her parents, falls in their driveway, is now suing them, suing her parents. In fact, when they heard about it, the Association of Trial Lawyers named her 'Woman of the Year.'"
